DMA_CLC

"DMA Clock Control Register"

AddressDMA_CLC_ADDR = 0xF0003C00
Absolute addressableYes
Reset value0x00000008
C typeDMA_CLC_t

DMA_CLC.bits "DMA Clock Control Register"
Mask:DMA_CLC_MASK = 0x0000001f
Masks:  DMA_CLC_<Bit field>_MASK
LSBs:DMA_CLC_<Bit field>_SHIFT
Bit field #Bits Bits' position Access Mask Description
DISR 1 0 - 0 rw 0x00000001 Module Disable Request Bit
DISS 1 1 - 1 r 0x00000002 Module Disable Status Bit
SPEN 1 2 - 2 rw 0x00000004 Module Suspend Enable for OCDS
ONE 1 3 - 3 rw 0x00000008
SBWE 1 4 - 4 w 0x00000010 Module Suspend Bit Write Enable for OCDS
 readable0x0000000f 
writeable0x0000001d
volatile0x00000000

DMA_TRSR

"DMA Transaction Request State Register"

AddressDMA_TRSR_ADDR = 0xF0003C14
Absolute addressableYes
Reset value0x00000000
C typeDMA_TRSR_t

DMA_TRSR.bits "DMA Transaction Request State Register"
Mask:DMA_TRSR_MASK = 0xffffffff
Masks:  DMA_TRSR_<Bit field>_MASK
LSBs:DMA_TRSR_<Bit field>_SHIFT
Bit field #Bits Bits' position Access Mask Description
CH00 1 0 - 0 rh 0x00000001 Transaction Request State of DMA Channel 0n
0 No DMA request is pending for channel 0n.
1 A DMA request is pending for channel 0n.
CH01 1 1 - 1 rh 0x00000002 Transaction Request State of DMA Channel 0n
0 No DMA request is pending for channel 0n.
1 A DMA request is pending for channel 0n.
CH02 1 2 - 2 rh 0x00000004 Transaction Request State of DMA Channel 0n
0 No DMA request is pending for channel 0n.
1 A DMA request is pending for channel 0n.
CH03 1 3 - 3 rh 0x00000008 Transaction Request State of DMA Channel 0n
0 No DMA request is pending for channel 0n.
1 A DMA request is pending for channel 0n.
CH04 1 4 - 4 rh 0x00000010 Transaction Request State of DMA Channel 0n
0 No DMA request is pending for channel 0n.
1 A DMA request is pending for channel 0n.
CH05 1 5 - 5 rh 0x00000020 Transaction Request State of DMA Channel 0n
0 No DMA request is pending for channel 0n.
1 A DMA request is pending for channel 0n.
CH06 1 6 - 6 rh 0x00000040 Transaction Request State of DMA Channel 0n
0 No DMA request is pending for channel 0n.
1 A DMA request is pending for channel 0n.
CH07 1 7 - 7 rh 0x00000080 Transaction Request State of DMA Channel 0n
0 No DMA request is pending for channel 0n.
1 A DMA request is pending for channel 0n.
CH10 1 8 - 8 rh 0x00000100 Transaction Request State of DMA Channel 1n
0 No DMA request is pending for channel 1n.
1 A DMA request is pending for channel 1n.
CH11 1 9 - 9 rh 0x00000200 Transaction Request State of DMA Channel 1n

1 DMA channel mn has a high channel priority

00 Shadow address register not used. Source and destination address register are written directly
01 Shadow address register used for source address buffering. When writing to SADRmx, the address is buffered in SHADRmx and transferred to SADRmx with the start of the next DMA transaction
10 Shadow address register used for destination address buffering. When writing to DADRmx, the address is buffered in SHADRmx and transferred to DADRmx with the start of the next DMA transaction
11 Reserved
SHWEN 1 18 - 18 rw 0x00040000 Shadow Address Register Write Enable
0 Shadow address register is read only and the value stored in the SHADRmx is automatically set to 00000000H when the shadow transfer takes place
1 Shadow address register SHADRmx can be read and can be directly written. The value stored in the SHADRmx is not automatically modified when the shadow transfer takes place

CHMODE 1 20 - 20 rw 0x00100000 Channel Operation Mode
0 Single Mode operation is selected for DMA channel mn. After a transaction, DMA channel mn is disabled for further hardware requests (TRSR.HTREmn is reset by hardware) TRSR.HTREmn must be set again by software for starting a new transaction.
1 Continuous Mode operation is selected for DMA channel mn. After a transaction, bit TRSR.HTREmn remains set

1 Continuous Mode operation is selected for DMA channel mn. After a transaction, bit TRSR.HTREmn remains set

10 Shadow address register used for destination address buffering. When writing to DADRmx, the address is buffered in SHADRmx and transferred to DADRmx with the start of the next DMA transaction
11 Reserved

1 Shadow address register SHADRmx can be read and can be directly written. The value stored in the SHADRmx is not automatically modified when the shadow transfer takes place

1 TRSR.CHmn is reset when CHSRmn.TCOUNT=0 after a transfer. One transfer request starts a complete DMA transaction
CHMODE 1 20 - 20 rw 0x00100000 Channel Operation Mode
0 Single Mode operation is selected for DMA channel mn. After a transaction, DMA channel mn is disabled for further hardware requests (TRSR.HTREmn is reset by hardware) TRSR.HTREmn must be set again by software for starting a new transaction.
1 Continuous Mode operation is selected for DMA channel mn. After a transaction, bit TRSR.HTREmn remains set

00 8-bit (byte) data width for moves selected
01 16-bit (half-word) data width for moves selected

TCOUNT 10 0 - 9 rh 0x000003ff Transfer Count Status

DMA_CHCR15

"DMA Channel 15 Control Register"

AddressDMA_CHCR15_ADDR = 0xF0003E24
Absolute addressableYes
Reset value0x00000000
C typeDMA_CHCRm_t

DMA_CHCR15.bits "DMA Channel 15 Control Register"
Mask:DMA_CHCRm_MASK = 0xd37ff3ff
Masks:  DMA_CHCRm_<Bit field>_MASK
LSBs:DMA_CHCRm_<Bit field>_SHIFT
Bit field #Bits Bits' position Access Mask Description
TREL 10 0 - 9 rw 0x000003ff Transfer Reload Value
PRSEL 4 12 - 15 rw 0x0000f000 Peripheral Request Select
0000 Input CHmn_REQI0 selected
0001 Input CHmn_REQI1 selected
0010 Input CHmn_REQI2 selected
0011 Input CHmn_REQI3 selected
0100 Input CHmn_REQI4 selected
0101 Input CHmn_REQI5 selected
0110 Input CHmn_REQI6 selected
0111 Input CHmn_REQI7 selected
1000 Input CHmn_REQI8 selected
1001 Input CHmn_REQI9 selected
1010 Input CHmn_REQI10 selected
1011 Input CHmn_REQI11 selected
1100 Input CHmn_REQI12 selected
1101 Input CHmn_REQI13 selected
1110 Input CHmn_REQI14 selected
1111 Input CHmn_REQI15 selected
BLKM 3 16 - 18 rw 0x00070000 Block Mode
000 One DMA transfer has 1 DMA move
001 One DMA transfer has 2 DMA move
010 One DMA transfer has 4 DMA move
011 One DMA transfer has 8 DMA move
100 One DMA transfer has 16 DMA move
RROAT 1 19 - 19 rw 0x00080000 Reset Request Only After Transaction
0 TRSR.CHmn is reset after each transfer. A transfer request is required for each transfer.
1 TRSR.CHmn is reset when CHSRmn.TCOUNT=0 after a transfer. One transfer request starts a complete DMA transaction
CHMODE 1 20 - 20 rw 0x00100000 Channel Operation Mode
0 Single Mode operation is selected for DMA channel mn. After a transaction, DMA channel mn is disabled for further hardware requests (TRSR.HTREmn is reset by hardware) TRSR.HTREmn must be set again by software for starting a new transaction.
1 Continuous Mode operation is selected for DMA channel mn. After a transaction, bit TRSR.HTREmn remains set
CHDW 2 21 - 22 rw 0x00600000 Channel Data Width
00 8-bit (byte) data width for moves selected
01 16-bit (half-word) data width for moves selected
10 32-bit (word) data width for moves selected
11 Reserved
PATSEL 2 24 - 25 rw 0x03000000 Pattern Select
CHPRIO 1 28 - 28 rw 0x10000000 Channel Priority
0 DMA channel mn has a low channel priority
1 DMA channel mn has a high channel priority
DMAPRIO 2 30 - 31 rw 0xc0000000 DMA Priority
00 Low priority selected
01 Medium priority selected
10 Reserved
11 High priority selected
 readable0xd37ff3ff 
writeable0xd37ff3ff
volatile0x00000000

DMA_CHICR15

"DMA Channel 15 Interrupt Control Register"

AddressDMA_CHICR15_ADDR = 0xF0003E28
Absolute addressableYes
Reset value0x00000000
C typeDMA_CHICRm_t

DMA_CHICR15.bits "DMA Channel 15 Interrupt Control Register"
Mask:DMA_CHICRm_MASK = 0x0000ffff
Masks:  DMA_CHICRm_<Bit field>_MASK
LSBs:DMA_CHICRm_<Bit field>_SHIFT
Bit field #Bits Bits' position Access Mask Description
WRPSE 1 0 - 0 rw 0x00000001 Wrap Source Enable
0 Wrap source buffer interrupt disabled
1 Wrap source buffer interrupt enabled
WRPDE 1 1 - 1 rw 0x00000002 Wrap Destination Enable
0 Wrap destination buffer interrupt disabled
1 Wrap destination buffer interrupt enabled
INTCT 2 2 - 3 rw 0x0000000c Interrupt Control
00 No interrupt will be generated on changing the TCOUNT value. The bit INTSR.ICHmx is set when TCOUNT equals IRDV.
01 No interrupt will be generated on changing the TCOUNT value. The bit INTSR.ICHmx is set when TCOUNT is decremented
10 An interrupt is generated and bit INTSR.ICHmx is set each time TCOUNT equals IRDV
11 Interrupt is generated and bit INTSR.ICHmx is set each time TCOUNT is decremented
WRPP 4 4 - 7 rw 0x000000f0 Wrap Pointer
0000 SR0 selected for channel mx wrap buffer interrupt
0001 SR1 selected for channel mx wrap buffer interrupt
0010 SR2 selected for channel mx wrap buffer interrupt
0011 SR3 selected for channel mx wrap buffer interrupt
0100 SR4 selected for channel mx wrap buffer interrupt
0101 SR5 selected for channel mx wrap buffer interrupt
0110 SR6 selected for channel mx wrap buffer interrupt
0111 SR7 selected for channel mx wrap buffer interrupt
1000 SR8 selected for channel mx wrap buffer interrupt
1001 SR9 selected for channel mx wrap buffer interrupt
1010 SR10 selected for channel mx wrap buffer interrupt
1011 SR11 selected for channel mx wrap buffer interrupt
1100 SR12 selected for channel mx wrap buffer interrupt
1101 SR13 selected for channel mx wrap buffer interrupt
1110 SR14 selected for channel mx wrap buffer interrupt
1111 SR15 selected for channel mx wrap buffer interrupt
INTP 4 8 - 11 rw 0x00000f00 Interrupt Pointer
0000 SR0 selected for channel mx interrupt
0001 SR1 selected for channel mx interrupt
0010 SR2 selected for channel mx interrupt
0011 SR3 selected for channel mx interrupt
0100 SR4 selected for channel mx interrupt
0101 SR5 selected for channel mx interrupt
0110 SR6 selected for channel mx interrupt
0111 SR7 selected for channel mx interrupt
1000 SR8 selected for channel mx interrupt
1001 SR9 selected for channel mx interrupt
1010 SR10 selected for channel mx interrupt
1011 SR11 selected for channel mx interrupt
1100 SR12 selected for channel mx interrupt
1101 SR13 selected for channel mx interrupt
1110 SR14 selected for channel mx interrupt
1111 SR15 selected for channel mx interrupt
IRDV 4 12 - 15 rw 0x0000f000 Interrupt Raise Detect Value
 readable0x0000ffff 
writeable0x0000ffff
volatile0x00000000

DMA_ADRCR15

"DMA Channel 15 Address Control Register"

AddressDMA_ADRCR15_ADDR = 0xF0003E2C
Absolute addressableYes
Reset value0x00000000
C typeDMA_ADRCRm_t

DMA_ADRCR15.bits "DMA Channel 15 Address Control Register"
Mask:DMA_ADRCRm_MASK = 0x0007ffff
Masks:  DMA_ADRCRm_<Bit field>_MASK
LSBs:DMA_ADRCRm_<Bit field>_SHIFT
Bit field #Bits Bits' position Access Mask Description
SMF 3 0 - 2 rw 0x00000007 Source Address Modification Factor
000 Address offset is 1 xCHCRmx.CHDW
001 Address offset is 2 xCHCRmx.CHDW
010 Address offset is 4 xCHCRmx.CHDW
011 Address offset is 8 xCHCRmx.CHDW
100 Address offset is 16 xCHCRmx.CHDW
101 Address offset is 32 xCHCRmx.CHDW
110 Address offset is 64 xCHCRmx.CHDW
111 Address offset is 128 xCHCRmx.CHDW
INCS 1 3 - 3 rw 0x00000008 Increment of Source Address
0 Address offset will be subtracted
1 Address offset will be added.
DMF 3 4 - 6 rw 0x00000070 Destination Address Modification Factor
000 Address offset is 1 xCHDW
001 Address offset is 2 xCHDW
010 Address offset is 4 xCHDW
011 Address offset is 8 xCHDW
100 Address offset is 16 xCHDW
101 Address offset is 32 xCHDW
110 Address offset is 64 xCHDW
111 Address offset is 128 xCHDW
INCD 1 7 - 7 rw 0x00000080 Increment of Destination Address
0 Address offset will be subtracted
1 Address offset will be added
CBLS 4 8 - 11 rw 0x00000f00 Circular Buffer Length Source
0000 Source address SADR[31:0] is not updated
0001 Source address SADR[31:1] is not updated
0010 Source address SADR[31:2] is not updated
0011 Source address SADR[31:3] is not updated
... ...
1110 Source address SADR[31:14] is not updated
1111 Source address SADR[31:15] is not updated
CBLD 4 12 - 15 rw 0x0000f000 Circular Buffer Length Destination
0000 Destination address DADR[31:0] is not updated
0001 Destination address DADR[31:1] is not updated
0010 Destination address DADR[31:2] is not updated
0011 Destination address DADR[31:3] is not updated
... ...
1110 Destination address DADR[31:14] is not updated
1111 Destination address DADR[31:15] is not updated
SHCT 2 16 - 17 rw 0x00030000 Shadow Control
00 Shadow address register not used. Source and destination address register are written directly
01 Shadow address register used for source address buffering. When writing to SADRmx, the address is buffered in SHADRmx and transferred to SADRmx with the start of the next DMA transaction
10 Shadow address register used for destination address buffering. When writing to DADRmx, the address is buffered in SHADRmx and transferred to DADRmx with the start of the next DMA transaction
11 Reserved
SHWEN 1 18 - 18 rw 0x00040000 Shadow Address Register Write Enable
0 Shadow address register is read only and the value stored in the SHADRmx is automatically set to 00000000H when the shadow transfer takes place
1 Shadow address register SHADRmx can be read and can be directly written. The value stored in the SHADRmx is not automatically modified when the shadow transfer takes place
 readable0x0007ffff 
writeable0x0007ffff
volatile0x00000000

CHDW 2 21 - 22 rw 0x00600000 Channel Data Width
00 8-bit (byte) data width for moves selected
01 16-bit (half-word) data width for moves selected
10 32-bit (word) data width for moves selected
11 Reserved
PATSEL 2 24 - 25 rw 0x03000000 Pattern Select
CHPRIO 1 28 - 28 rw 0x10000000 Channel Priority
0 DMA channel mn has a low channel priority
1 DMA channel mn has a high channel priority
DMAPRIO 2 30 - 31 rw 0xc0000000 DMA Priority
00 Low priority selected
01 Medium priority selected
10 Reserved
11 High priority selected
 readable0xd37ff3ff 
writeable0xd37ff3ff
volatile0x00000000

01 No interrupt will be generated on changing the TCOUNT value. The bit INTSR.ICHmx is set when TCOUNT is decremented
10 An interrupt is generated and bit INTSR.ICHmx is set each time TCOUNT equals IRDV
11 Interrupt is generated and bit INTSR.ICHmx is set each time TCOUNT is decremented

DMA_ADRCR17

AddressDMA_ADRCR17_ADDR = 0xF0003E6C
Absolute addressableYes
Reset value0x00000000
C typeDMA_ADRCRm_t

DMA_ADRCR17.bits "DMA Channel 17 Address Control Register"
Mask:DMA_ADRCRm_MASK = 0x0007ffff
Masks:  DMA_ADRCRm_<Bit field>_MASK
LSBs:DMA_ADRCRm_<Bit field>_SHIFT
Bit field #Bits Bits' position Access Mask Description
SMF 3 0 - 2 rw 0x00000007 Source Address Modification Factor
000 Address offset is 1 xCHCRmx.CHDW
001 Address offset is 2 xCHCRmx.CHDW
010 Address offset is 4 xCHCRmx.CHDW
011 Address offset is 8 xCHCRmx.CHDW
100 Address offset is 16 xCHCRmx.CHDW
101 Address offset is 32 xCHCRmx.CHDW
110 Address offset is 64 xCHCRmx.CHDW
111 Address offset is 128 xCHCRmx.CHDW
INCS 1 3 - 3 rw 0x00000008 Increment of Source Address
0 Address offset will be subtracted
1 Address offset will be added.
DMF 3 4 - 6 rw 0x00000070 Destination Address Modification Factor
000 Address offset is 1 xCHDW
001 Address offset is 2 xCHDW
010 Address offset is 4 xCHDW
011 Address offset is 8 xCHDW
100 Address offset is 16 xCHDW
101 Address offset is 32 xCHDW
110 Address offset is 64 xCHDW
111 Address offset is 128 xCHDW
INCD 1 7 - 7 rw 0x00000080 Increment of Destination Address
0 Address offset will be subtracted
1 Address offset will be added
CBLS 4 8 - 11 rw 0x00000f00 Circular Buffer Length Source
0000 Source address SADR[31:0] is not updated
0001 Source address SADR[31:1] is not updated
0010 Source address SADR[31:2] is not updated
0011 Source address SADR[31:3] is not updated
... ...
1110 Source address SADR[31:14] is not updated
1111 Source address SADR[31:15] is not updated
CBLD 4 12 - 15 rw 0x0000f000 Circular Buffer Length Destination
0000 Destination address DADR[31:0] is not updated
0001 Destination address DADR[31:1] is not updated
0010 Destination address DADR[31:2] is not updated
0011 Destination address DADR[31:3] is not updated
... ...
1110 Destination address DADR[31:14] is not updated
1111 Destination address DADR[31:15] is not updated
SHCT 2 16 - 17 rw 0x00030000 Shadow Control
00 Shadow address register not used. Source and destination address register are written directly
01 Shadow address register used for source address buffering. When writing to SADRmx, the address is buffered in SHADRmx and transferred to SADRmx with the start of the next DMA transaction
10 Shadow address register used for destination address buffering. When writing to DADRmx, the address is buffered in SHADRmx and transferred to DADRmx with the start of the next DMA transaction
11 Reserved
SHWEN 1 18 - 18 rw 0x00040000 Shadow Address Register Write Enable
0 Shadow address register is read only and the value stored in the SHADRmx is automatically set to 00000000H when the shadow transfer takes place
1 Shadow address register SHADRmx can be read and can be directly written. The value stored in the SHADRmx is not automatically modified when the shadow transfer takes place
